### Task 6.1 — `planDocuments.ts` parser

Markdown + YAML frontmatter parser. Schema per spec §6.1:

```ts
interface PlanDocument {
  planId: string;
  title: string;
  status: 'draft' | 'active' | 'paused' | 'done';
  planType?: 'feature' | 'bug' | 'refactor' | 'research';
  priority?: 'urgent' | 'high' | 'normal' | 'low';
  owner?: string;
  stakeholders?: string[];
  tags?: string[];
  created?: string;
  updated?: string;
  progress?: number;
  agentSessions: AgentSessionRef[];
  objective: string;
  acceptanceCriteria: ChecklistItem[];
  outOfScope?: string[];
  context?: string;
}
```

`parsePlanDocument(filepath)` reads file, splits frontmatter (delimited by `---`), parses YAML via `yaml` npm package, parses body sections by `##` headings (Objective, Acceptance Criteria, Out of Scope, Context). `planId` derived from `sha1(filepath + frontmatter.title)`.

Test: parses spec/2026-05-21-apohara-v1-design.md OK; rejects malformed frontmatter; extracts acceptance criteria as `[{checked: false, text: "..."}]`.

### Task 6.2 — `planStatusCache.ts` bounded read + SHA cache

Per spec §6.2. Cache map `{filepath: {plan, mtime, sha}}`. `getFast(filepath)`: stat file; if mtime matches cache, return cached; else bounded read 4KB (frontmatter only), compute SHA, compare to cached SHA. If SHA matches, extend cache mtime + return cached plan. Else full parse.

Test: doesn't reparse when frontmatter unchanged; reparses on body change.

### Task 6.3 — `watcher.ts` file watcher → Tauri events

Per spec §6.3. `chokidar.watch(rootPath + '/**/*.md')`. On `change`/`add`/`unlink`, invalidate cache + emit `apohara://plan-changed` / `apohara://plan-added` / `apohara://plan-removed` via `listenerRegistry.dispatch` (Task 1.18).

Test: file write → invalidates + emits event.

### Task 6.4 — `apohara auto --spec` CLI flag

Modify `src/cli.ts`. Add `--spec <path>` flag to `auto` subcommand. When provided: load plan via `planDocuments.parsePlanDocument`, validate `status !== 'paused'` (fail with `ApoharaError SPEC_PAUSED`), build `ObjectivePayload` from plan, call existing `auto` flow with payload. After run completes, append agent session ref to plan's `planStatus.agentSessions` via auto-managed `<!-- apohara:agentSessions:start --> ... <!-- apohara:agentSessions:end -->` block (safe rewrite preserves rest of file).

Test: `apohara auto --spec docs/superpowers/specs/2026-05-21-apohara-v1-design.md` produces same DAG as text prompt mode (placeholder — full coverage in Stage 10 integration test).

### Task 6.5 — Roster hardening: real legacy roster

Modify `src/core/providers/legacy-roster.ts` (replaces Stage 3 placeholder). List the 22 legacy providers: 21 cloud (`anthropic-api`, `openai-api`, `groq`, `together`, `mistral`, `openrouter`, `cohere`, `gemini-api`, `gemini-oauth`, etc.) + `gemini-cli` driver. Each as a thin subclass of `BaseAgentProvider` that throws on spawn ("legacy provider — Stage 6 implementation stub").

UI picker (Stage 7) filters by `getActiveProviders()` result. Setting `APOHARA_LEGACY_PROVIDERS=1` surfaces them.

Documentation: CHANGELOG.md gets the rationale ("Roster hardened to 3 CLI drivers for TOS safety. Legacy providers stay behind APOHARA_LEGACY_PROVIDERS=1 — see docs/PROVIDER_PATTERNS.md.").

### Task 6.6 — Stage 6 verification

```bash
bun test tests/core/spec/
bun test tests/core/providers/roster.test.ts
git tag stage-6-spec-roster
git commit --allow-empty -m "chore: Stage 6 (SPEC.md + Roster hardening) complete"
```

## Stage 7 — UI: TaskBoard + Plans + Permissions + Timeline

**Goal:** Build the desktop UI surface. TaskBoard kanban with modular hooks-per-concern; PlansPanel sidebar; PermissionDialog (durable, render-from-ledger); Verification Timeline trust theater; custom tool widgets registry.

**Files in this stage:**
- Create: `packages/desktop/src/components/TaskBoard/{TaskBoard,TaskBoardLane,TaskBoardCard,TaskBoardDrawer,TaskBoardColumnHeader,PlansPanel,AgentConfigPanel}.tsx`
- Create: `packages/desktop/src/components/TaskBoard/hooks/{use-taskboard-pointer-drag,use-taskboard-area-selection,use-taskboard-shift-wheel-scroll,use-taskboard-column-resize,use-taskboard-outside-dismiss,use-taskboard-selection,use-taskboard-smart-attention,use-taskboard-store}.ts`
- Create: `packages/desktop/src/components/PermissionDialog.tsx` (renders from ledger event)
- Create: `packages/desktop/src/components/VerificationTimeline.tsx` (trust theater: lock acquired → agent acted → judge scored → critic scored → ledger entry hashed)
- Create: `packages/desktop/src/components/ToolWidgets/registry.ts` (custom widgets keyed by tool name)
- Create: `packages/desktop/src/components/ToolWidgets/{EditWidget,BashWidget,LedgerReadWidget}.tsx`
- Create: `packages/desktop/src/store/listeners/{runListeners,taskListeners,verifierListeners,hookListeners,planListeners}.ts`
- Modify: `packages/desktop/src/App.tsx` (mount ViewToggle Graph/Board, register listeners at boot)

**Approach:** Each subsection is a single React component or hook. Tests use Playwright (already in repo per spec §17.10). The 28 tasks all follow the same pattern: write spec (`.spec.ts`) → mount component in test fixture → assert behavior.

### Task 7.1 — TaskBoard skeleton + use-taskboard-store hook (compressed)

Single-file component with `<TaskBoardLane>` × N columns. Status enum from spec §4: `pending | ready | dispatched | in_verification | done | failed | blocked + custom[]`. `use-taskboard-store` selects from the **same store** as the DAG canvas (regla CRÍTICA del spec) via `useDagStore(state => state.tasks)`.

Test: mount TaskBoard → verify 7 columns render → verify task ID appears in `pending` lane when DAG store has a pending task.

### Task 7.2 — TaskBoardCard with agent icon + worktree slug + cost ticker

Renders per spec §4: title, agent icon (Claude/Codex/OpenCode), worktree slug, duration, cost (USD + tokens). Blocked reason shown when `task.status === 'blocked'` (overlap_symbols + waiting_for). Force fail button with confirm dialog → calls `apohara orchestration task-update <id> --status failed`.

### Task 7.3 — Hooks: pointer-drag, area-selection, shift-wheel-scroll, column-resize, outside-dismiss

5 separate hooks per spec §4 (modular hooks-per-concern of orca #15). Each hook is testable in isolation. Pointer-drag uses native pointer events (no HTML5 DnD). Shift-wheel-scroll converts vertical wheel to horizontal scroll on the canvas.

### Task 7.4 — use-taskboard-smart-attention 4-tier classifier

Per spec §4 + culture #3 (apohara-attention crate). Classifies each task into `NeedsYou | Done | Working | Idle`. Default sort by class then attentionTimestamp. Hook authority per-pane (not per-worktree). Min-of-pane-classes promotion (most urgent pane bumps the worktree class).

### Task 7.5 — TaskBoardDrawer with hook events + verdict + lineage

Click on card → drawer slides in. Shows: spec (description + symbols), hook events (virtual list of `pre_tool_use`/`post_tool_use`/`stop`), verification mesh decisions (judge + critic + INV-15 status), decision gates (opened by this task + blocking this task), worktree info (path, branch, dirty/clean, commits ahead/behind), ledger replay button.

### Task 7.6 — PlansPanel sidebar

Per spec §6. Lists plan documents discovered by Task 6.3 watcher. Filters by `planStatus` / priority / owner / tags. Click → opens SPEC.md in Monaco. Each plan shows `agentSessions` with status + click-to-jump.

### Task 7.7 — AgentConfigPanel sidebar

Per spec §4. For each active agent: shows MCP config resolved (Task 6.5.1 from Stage 8), permissions in effect (Task 5.3), capabilities (Task 3.1 + 4.5.1). Read-only during a run; edit-mode only when no run active.

### Task 7.8 — ViewToggle Graph/Board in top bar

Per spec §4. `<ViewToggle views={["graph", "board"]} current={currentView} onChange={setCurrentView} />`. Both views read from the same store.

### Task 7.9 — PermissionDialog renders from ledger event (DURABLE per spec §4.6)

Per spec §4.6 + nimbalyst #3.1. Subscribes via centralized listener to `apohara://permission-request` (from ledger). Modal dialog shows tool + input + scope options (once / session / always). On user click, emits `apohara://permission-response` event → writes `permission_response` to ledger. Replay reconstructs both events.

CRITICAL: NEVER store dialog state in local React `useState` — always derive from ledger. Test: unmount + remount → dialog reappears with same content.

### Task 7.10 — VerificationTimeline trust theater

Per spec §4 + nimbalyst.com finding #15. Renders a linear timeline of verification steps: `lock_acquired → agent_acted → judge_scored → critic_scored → ledger_entry_hashed`. Each step has a status icon (pending / in_progress / done / failed). Converts invisible guarantee (ledger hash chain) into visible trust theater.

Test: simulate full run end-to-end → all 5 timeline nodes light up in order.

### Task 7.11 — Custom tool widgets registry

Per spec §4 + nimbalyst #7.3. `ToolWidgets/registry.ts` maps tool names to React components:
- `Edit` / `Write` → Monaco diff widget
- `Bash` → terminal-styled output
- `mcp__apohara__read_ledger` → virtual table
- `mcp__apohara__list_runs` → list with sparkline per run

Fallback: generic JSON pretty-print for unregistered tools.

Auto-handles MCP prefix (`mcp__apohara__*`).

### Task 7.12 — Centralized IPC listeners at boot

Per spec §0.1. `packages/desktop/src/store/listeners/index.ts` exposes `registerAllListeners()` called once in `App.tsx` startup. Wires up listeners for `apohara://run-started`, `apohara://task-completed`, `apohara://verifier-conflict`, `apohara://ledger-event`, `apohara://hook-event`, `apohara://plan-changed`, `apohara://permission-request`. Each listener mutates atoms.

### Task 7.13 — E2E Playwright tests

Per spec §4 + spec §7. Tests in `packages/desktop/tests/e2e/`:
- `taskboard_toggle_graph_board.spec.ts`
- `force_fail_preserves_worktree.spec.ts`
- `multi_select_bulk_archive.spec.ts`
- `smart_attention_sort.spec.ts`
- `plans_panel_filter.spec.ts`
- `custom_column.spec.ts`
- `durable_permission_dialog_survives_remount.spec.ts`
- `verification_timeline_completes.spec.ts`

### Task 7.14 — Stage 7 verification

```bash
bun run --filter @apohara/desktop e2e
git tag stage-7-ui
git commit --allow-empty -m "chore: Stage 7 (UI: TaskBoard + Plans + Permissions + Timeline) complete"
```

## Stage 8 — Internal MCP servers + MCP Config Adapter

**Goal:** 4 internal MCP servers (`apohara.ledger`, `apohara.runs`, `apohara.indexer`, `apohara.settings`) with bearer-token auth + audit log. MCP Config Adapter Pattern (canonical → 6 dialects).

**Files in this stage:**
- Create: `src/core/mcp/servers/{apohara-ledger,apohara-runs,apohara-indexer,apohara-settings}.ts`
- Create: `src/core/mcp/base/{McpServer,auditLogger,rateLimit}.ts`
- Create: `src/core/mcp/bootstrap.ts`
- Create: `crates/apohara-mcp-bridge/src/lib.rs` (real implementation replacing Stage 1 placeholder)
- Create: `crates/apohara-mcp-bridge/src/adapters/{claude,codex,opencode,gemini,cursor,copilot}.rs`
- Create: `crates/apohara-mcp-bridge/default_mcp.json` (canonical config)

### Task 8.1 — Base McpServer + bearer auth + audit logger + rate limit

`src/core/mcp/base/McpServer.ts`: Bun.serve()-based MCP server (SSE transport). Bearer token middleware (Authorization: Bearer X). Each tool call → audit logger writes to apohara-audit JSONL (Task 1.9). Rate limiter: token bucket per-server (30/min, 200/hour).

Test: requests without bearer → 401; valid bearer → tool dispatches + audit entry written; rate limit triggers 429 after 31st call/min.

### Task 8.2 — `apohara.ledger` MCP server

Tools: `read_events(runId, types?, offset?, limit?)`, `replay_run(runId)`, `get_last_event(runId, type)`, `search_events(runId, query)` (FTS over payload).

Test: spawn server → MCP client calls `read_events("r-1", [], 0, 10)` → receives ledger events from runs table.

### Task 8.3 — `apohara.runs` MCP server

Tools: `list_runs(filter?: {status?, since?, limit?})`, `inspect_run(runId)`, `get_current_run()`, `get_run_diff(runId)`.

Test: insert runs → `list_runs({limit:5})` returns 5 most recent.

### Task 8.4 — `apohara.indexer` MCP server (proxy to Rust)

Tools: `blast_radius(symbol)`, `search_symbols(query, kind?)`, `file_symbols(file)`, `reverse_dependencies(symbol)`.

Internally opens UDS to `apohara-indexer` (existing crate). Stage 4.18 confirmed pathsafety integration; this just wraps queries.

Test: query symbol → response forwarded from indexer subprocess.

### Task 8.5 — `apohara.settings` MCP server with allow/deny/rate-limit/audit

Tools: `get_setting(key)`, `set_setting(key, value)`, `list_settings()`.

ALLOWLIST: `ui.theme`, `ui.density`, `roster.preferred`, `cost.dailyBudget`.
DENYLIST: `providers.apiKeys`, `providers.oauth`, `github.appPrivateKey`.
RATE: 30/min, 200/hour.
AUDIT: each set_setting → ledger event.

Kill switch: `process.env.APOHARA_MCP_SETTINGS_DISABLED=1` → server doesn't start.

Test: deny-listed key returns 403; rate limit kicks in; audit entry persists.

### Task 8.6 — `bootstrap.ts` starts all 4 servers + writes endpoint file

Generates random bearer token (16 bytes hex). Allocates 4 free ports. Starts each server on its port. Writes `~/.apohara/sockets/mcp-endpoints.json` with `{token, servers: {ledger, runs, indexer, settings}}` (atomic write).

Hooks installer (Task 2.6) reads endpoint file when generating per-spawn MCP config.

### Task 8.7 — `apohara-mcp-bridge` real crate (canonical → 6 dialects)

Replace Stage 1.14 placeholder. Rust crate with:
- `default_mcp.json` (canonical config — JSON array of `{name, meta, command, args, env, type}`)
- `src/adapters/{claude,codex,opencode,...}.rs` — pure functions converting canonical to provider-native shape

Claude: `{ mcpServers: { name: { command, args, env } } }` in `.claude/mcp.json`.
Codex: `[mcp_servers.NAME] command="..."; args=[...]` in `.codex/config.toml`.
OpenCode: `{ mcp: { name: { type: "local"|"remote", command, args, env } } }` in `.opencode/settings.json`.

Use JSONC parser (jsonc-parser crate per spec §0.27) to preserve comments in destination files.

Test: roundtrip canonical → claude → parse back → identical canonical (modulo provider-specific extensions).

### Task 8.8 — MCP config injection in spawn

Modify `BaseAgentProvider.spawn` (Task 3.9): after applying trust preset, call `apohara-mcp-bridge::adapt(provider, canonical)` → write to provider-native config path. Claude gets `.claude/mcp.json` in the worktree; Codex gets env var `CODEX_MCP_SERVERS_JSON`; OpenCode gets flag `--mcp-config-path`.

Test: spawn → verify mcp.json appears in workspace with `apohara.ledger` server registered.

### Task 8.9 — Stage 8 verification

```bash
bun test tests/core/mcp/
cargo test -p apohara-mcp-bridge
git tag stage-8-mcp
git commit --allow-empty -m "chore: Stage 8 (Internal MCP servers + Config Adapter) complete"
```

## Stage 9 — github-bridge (poll-only)

**Goal:** GitHub Issues with `apohara` label → orchestration DB tasks → PR with replay link. GitHub App auth (no PAT). Idempotency key embedded in PR body.

**Files in this stage:**
- Create: `packages/github-bridge/src/{index,poller,issue-parser,pr-builder,github-app-auth,octokit-client}.ts`
- Create: `packages/github-bridge/src/webhook.ts` (stub returning 501 for v1.0)
- Create: `docs/github-app-setup.md`
- Create: `tests/integration/github-bridge-e2e.test.ts`

### Task 9.1 — GitHub App auth (no PAT)

`github-app-auth.ts`: reads `APOHARA_GITHUB_APP_ID` + `APOHARA_GITHUB_APP_PRIVATE_KEY_PATH` env vars. Generates JWT for app authentication; exchanges for installation token; caches token with TTL 50min (refresh proactively at 50min, expires at 60min).

Test: stub octokit auth endpoints → roundtrip JWT → installation token.

### Task 9.2 — Octokit client with retry + rate-limit

`octokit-client.ts`: wraps `@octokit/rest` with exponential backoff on 5xx + rate-limit-aware (reads `x-ratelimit-remaining` header).

### Task 9.3 — Issue parser

`issue-parser.ts` per spec §5: detect SPEC.md inline (frontmatter or `## SPEC` heading) → parse via `planDocuments.parsePlanDocument` (Task 6.1). Else parse as plain (first paragraph = objective, checklist sections = acceptance criteria).

Returns `ParseResult = { kind: 'objective', payload } | { kind: 'ambiguous', missing: [...] }`.

### Task 9.4 — Poller (Bun.cron every 60s)

`poller.ts`: `octokit.list_issues({label: 'apohara', state: 'open'})` → for each unprocessed (cross-check orchestration DB messages table for `from='@github'` with `issue_id` payload) → `issue-parser.parse(body)` → if ambiguous, `octokit.create_comment(issue, "needs clarification: ...")` + add `apohara-needs-input` label; else `insertTask(db, {...})` from Task 2.10 + add `apohara-in-progress` label.

### Task 9.5 — PR builder with idempotency key

`pr-builder.ts` per spec §5.1: builds PR body with template (Apohara header + Run ID + agents + verification + replay link + changes summary + INV-15 status). Embeds `<!-- apohara-attempt: sha256:abc... -->` HTML comment for retry-safe idempotency.

Before creating PR, checks for existing by:
1. `findPRByIdempotencyKey(repo, key)` — looks for the HTML comment
2. `findPRByHeadBranch(repo, head)` — fallback by head branch name
3. `findLinkedPRs(repo, issue_num)` — regex match `close[sd]?|fix(?:e[sd])?` + `#issueNum`

If existing + still open → update body. If existing + merged → return as-is. Else → create new.

### Task 9.6 — webhook.ts stub (501 for v1.0)

`webhook.ts`: HTTP endpoint that always returns 501 Not Implemented. Reserves the path for v1.1+ webhook delivery worker integration.

### Task 9.7 — `docs/github-app-setup.md`

Step-by-step for users:
1. Create GitHub App at https://github.com/settings/apps/new
2. Manifest JSON (paste):
```json
{
  "name": "Apohara Orchestrator",
  "url": "https://apohara.dev",
  "hook_attributes": { "url": "https://your-host/apohara-webhook" },
  "redirect_url": "https://apohara.dev/setup",
  "callback_urls": ["https://apohara.dev/auth/callback"],
  "default_permissions": {
    "issues": "write",
    "pull_requests": "write",
    "contents": "read"
  },
  "default_events": ["issues", "issue_comment"]
}
```
3. Install on your repo(s)
4. Generate private key → save to `~/.apohara/github-app.private-key.pem`
5. Set env: `APOHARA_GITHUB_APP_ID=...` + `APOHARA_GITHUB_APP_PRIVATE_KEY_PATH=~/.apohara/github-app.private-key.pem`
6. Run `apohara provider doctor github` (Stage 10) to verify

### Task 9.8 — E2E test with mock Octokit

`tests/integration/github-bridge-e2e.test.ts`: mock @octokit/rest. Simulate issue with `apohara` label → poller picks up → orchestration DB has task → scheduler completes run (mocked agents) → pr-builder creates PR → assert PR body contains `<!-- apohara-attempt: -->` marker + replay link.

### Task 9.9 — Stage 9 verification

```bash
bun test packages/github-bridge/
bun test tests/integration/github-bridge-e2e.test.ts
git tag stage-9-github-bridge
git commit --allow-empty -m "chore: Stage 9 (github-bridge poll-only) complete"
```

## Stage 10 — Integration tests + Setup verification

**Goal:** 11 integration tests covering all subsystems end-to-end. Setup verification gate (`apohara verify-setup` enrolls a seed task that exercises the full pipeline). Doctor with plan-compile checks.

**Files in this stage:**
- Create: `tests/fixtures/sample-monorepo/` (realistic TS+Rust monorepo for tests)
- Create: `tests/integration/` (10 named tests per spec §7)
- Create: `src/core/orchestration/setup-verification.ts` (enroll LOCAL-SETUP-001)
- Create: `src/cli/doctor.ts` (full doctor command with sections + plan-compile dry-run)

### Task 10.1 — Realistic fixture workspace

`tests/fixtures/sample-monorepo/` per spec §7. Structure:
```
sample-monorepo/
├── packages/api/         (mini Express TS service)
│   ├── src/routes/{users,auth}.ts
│   ├── src/db/schema.ts
│   └── package.json
├── packages/shared/      (shared types)
├── crates/parser/        (mini Rust crate)
│   ├── src/lib.rs
│   └── Cargo.toml
├── docs/plans/sample-plan.md  (SPEC.md de demo)
├── package.json + bun.lockb
└── Cargo.toml
```

Each integration test does `fs.cp(fixture, tmpdir)` then operates in the copy.

### Task 10.2 — Integration test #1: worktree isolation parallel

`tests/integration/worktree_isolation_parallel.test.ts`: copy fixture; create two tasks with non-overlapping manifests (writes `packages/api/src/routes/users.ts::getUsers` vs `packages/api/src/routes/auth.ts::login`); start run; assert both dispatched at same tick.

### Task 10.3 — Integration test #2: worktree isolation serial via decision_gate

Two tasks with overlap (writes `createUser`, reads `createUser`); assert second goes to `blocked` with `decision_gate` open; mark first completed; assert second unblocks next tick.

### Task 10.4 — Integration test #3: github-bridge e2e (mock octokit)

Mock @octokit/rest; simulate issue → assert task in DB → mock agents complete → assert PR body contains attempt key + replay link.

### Task 10.5 — Integration test #4: spec parser out-of-scope propagation

`tests/integration/spec_parser_out_of_scope.test.ts`: SPEC.md with `## Out of Scope: no authentication` → decomposer respects (no auth tasks generated). Verify against fixture monorepo.

### Task 10.6 — Integration test #5: kanban/DAG sync

Mount TaskBoard + SwarmCanvas in test harness; modify task via scheduler API; assert both views update.

### Task 10.7 — Integration test #6: agent-hooks integration

Spawn fake CLI process; trigger hook script via curl; assert message inserted in orchestration DB + Tauri event broadcast.

### Task 10.8 — Integration test #7: ContextForge regression (CRITICAL — 310/310 stays green)

`tests/integration/contextforge_regression.test.ts`: `cd apohara-context-forge && PYTHONPATH=. pytest tests/ -q` → assert exit 0 + "310 passed".

If this fails, ENTIRE pipeline blocks. This is the V-1 acceptance criterion.

### Task 10.9 — Integration test #8: ledger SHA chain replay-verifies after canonical projection

Load fixture run from `tests/fixtures/replay-runs/r-001.jsonl` → apply canonical projector (Stage 2.x) → verify SHA chain still validates via `apohara replay --verify`.

### Task 10.10 — Integration test #9: provider refactor no regression

Spawn each of the 3 CLI drivers (claude / codex / opencode) via BaseAgentProvider; assert each returns SpawnedSession without errors. (Real CLI bin not required in CI — use stub protocols from Task 3.10.)

### Task 10.11 — Integration test #10: permission bash compound never approves with "always"

Request `Bash(git status:*)` permission as `always` scope; force compound `git status && rm -rf /`; assert prompt forced to `once` scope.

### Task 10.12 — Integration test #11: internal MCP e2e

Spawn fake claude with mcp.json pointing at `apohara.runs` server; call `list_runs` tool; receive response; assert audit log entry written.

### Task 10.13 — Setup verification task (LOCAL-SETUP-001)

`src/core/orchestration/setup-verification.ts`: `enrollSetupVerificationTask(db)` inserts `LOCAL-SETUP-001` per spec §7.1 with description "Setup verification: each enabled provider must echo 'apohara-ok-{provider}' to its session, judge must approve." Scheduler treats it as low-priority lane (only runs when no normal-runnable tasks).

`apohara verify-setup` CLI command: enroll task + wait for completion + assert verdict approved + ledger_root valid → exit 0 if all OK, else exit 1 with diagnostic.

### Task 10.14 — `apohara doctor` with sections + plan-compile dry-run

`src/cli/doctor.ts` per spec §7.1. Sections:
- `runtime` — Bun version, Rust version, candle available
- `roster` — providers reachable (CLI binaries on PATH + `--version` works)
- `policy` — for each (runner, preset) combo: compile dry-run plan; assert validateRunnerPolicyPlan passes
- `sandbox` — apohara-sandbox crate compiles + seccomp filter installs
- `ledger` — DB writable, hash chain verifies, replay round-trips
- `mcp` — 4 servers respond to /health on their assigned ports
- `assigned` — LOCAL-SETUP-001 visible in /tasks/mine?status=in_progress (or completed)

Flags: `--skip-<section>` (CI partial), `--json` (machine-readable for CI gates).

Output format (text mode):
```
[runtime    ] ✅ Bun 1.3.13 · Rust 1.95.0
[roster     ] ✅ claude (1.4.2) · codex (0.5.1) · opencode (--pure)
[policy     ] ✅ runner-policy balanced compiles for all 3 providers
[sandbox    ] ✅ apohara-sandbox 0.4.1 operational
[ledger     ] ✅ DB writable, chain verified (4 entries, root=sha256:abc...)
[mcp        ] ✅ apohara.ledger (8901) · apohara.runs (8902) · apohara.indexer (8903) · apohara.settings (8904)
[assigned   ] ✅ LOCAL-SETUP-001 verdict=Approved · ledger_root=sha256:abc123
✅ Apohara setup verified end-to-end.
```

### Task 10.15 — Stage 10 verification

```bash
bun test tests/integration/
git tag stage-10-integration
git commit --allow-empty -m "chore: Stage 10 (Integration tests + Setup verification) complete"
```

## Stage 11 — Release Phase 6

**Goal:** v1.0.0 release. Cross-OS binaries via GitHub-hosted runners. Homebrew formula. curl|sh install script. INV-15 paper v3.0 submitted to arXiv. README + ARCHITECTURE.md + CHANGELOG.md reflect v1.0.

**Files in this stage:**
- Modify: `.github/workflows/desktop-release.yml` (cross-OS matrix)
- Create: `.github/workflows/release-promote.yml` (pre-release → stable)
- Modify: `packaging/homebrew/apohara.rb` (template with `{{SHA256_*}}` placeholders)
- Modify: `scripts/install.sh` (production-ready)
- Create: `scripts/release-promote.sh` (alpha → stable flipper)
- Create: `scripts/two-track-events.ts` (SSE + webhook delivery worker)
- Modify: `README.md` (rewrite per nimbalyst.com guidance)
- Modify: `ARCHITECTURE.md` (reflect Stages 1-10 architecture)
- Modify: `CHANGELOG.md` (v1.0.0 entry)
- Create: `PRINCIPLES.md` (6-principle manifesto: Verifiability over vibes / Locks over hopes / Audit over trust / Local-first over cloud / Wrappers over keys / Formal over folklore)

### Task 11.1 — Validate `.github/workflows/desktop-release.yml` cross-OS matrix

Matrix per spec §8.1:
```yaml
strategy:
  matrix:
    include:
      - os: ubuntu-latest        # Linux x86_64 → AppImage, deb
      - os: macos-latest         # macOS arm64 → dmg
      - os: macos-13             # macOS x86_64 → dmg
      - os: windows-latest       # Windows x86_64 → msi
```

CRITICAL: when installing native deps cross-arch, single `bun install` with ALL optional deps — separate installs prune previous as "extraneous" (nimbalyst lesson).

Push tag `v1.0.0-rc.1` → workflow publishes pre-release to alpha channel.

### Task 11.2 — Two-track push events (SSE + webhook delivery worker)

Per spec §8.0. `src/server/sse-router.ts`: `GET /api/events/stream?eventTypes=...` → text/event-stream + `Last-Event-ID` resume.

`scripts/two-track-events.ts` (background daemon): webhook delivery worker with HMAC SHA-256 signing + 8 attempts back-off `[0,10,30,90,300,900,1800,3600]s` + 410 auto-disable. Subscriptions stored in orchestration DB.

CLI: `apohara webhook subscribe https://example.com/hook --events task:dispatched,worker_done --secret @secret.txt`.

### Task 11.3 — Pre-release → promote-to-stable flow

`scripts/release-promote.sh` per spec §8.2 + nimbalyst pattern: flips SAME release `prerelease: false` (no rebuild, no second tag). Rebuilds cumulative RELEASE_NOTES.md.

`apohara release promote v1.0.0` CLI wraps the script.

### Task 11.4 — Homebrew formula

`packaging/homebrew/apohara.rb` per spec §8.3:
```ruby
class Apohara < Formula
  desc "Verifiable multi-AI orchestrator for builders who don't want to manage API keys"
  homepage "https://github.com/SuarezPM/Apohara"
  version "1.0.0"
  on_macos do
    on_arm do
      url "https://github.com/SuarezPM/Apohara/releases/download/v1.0.0/Apohara-macOS-arm64.dmg"
      sha256 "{{SHA256_MACOS_ARM64}}"
    end
    on_intel do
      url "https://github.com/SuarezPM/Apohara/releases/download/v1.0.0/Apohara-macOS-x64.dmg"
      sha256 "{{SHA256_MACOS_X64}}"
    end
  end
  on_linux do
    url "https://github.com/SuarezPM/Apohara/releases/download/v1.0.0/Apohara-Linux.AppImage"
    sha256 "{{SHA256_LINUX}}"
  end
  def install
    bin.install "apohara"
  end
  test do
    system "#{bin}/apohara", "--version"
  end
end
```

CI tagger renders `{{SHA256_*}}` with real digests + pushes to `SuarezPM/homebrew-tap`.

### Task 11.5 — `curl|sh` install script

`scripts/install.sh` per spec §8.4: detects platform/arch (incl. Rosetta), fetches latest tag via GitHub API, downloads binary + SHA-256 checksum, verifies, installs to `${APOHARA_INSTALL_DIR:-$HOME/.local/bin}`.

Smoke test:
```bash
docker run --rm -i ubuntu:24.04 bash -c "apt-get update -qq && apt-get install -qq -y curl tar && curl -fsSL https://raw.githubusercontent.com/SuarezPM/Apohara/main/scripts/install.sh | sh && apohara --version"
```

Should print version. Add to release-blocking CI.

### Task 11.6 — README rewrite per nimbalyst.com guidance

Rewrite `README.md` per spec §8.3 + nimbalyst.com findings:

1. **Hero**: "The verifiable multi-AI orchestrator for builders who don't want to manage API keys" + tagline "For builders who ship"
2. **Download CTA**: 3-platform buttons (macOS/Windows/Linux)
3. **Pain → relief feature grid** (5 items):
   - "No more 'which agent broke main?'" → semantic locks + SHA-256 ledger
   - "No more API key juggling across machines" → CLI wrapper providers
   - "No more 'the judge agreed with itself'" → dual-arbiter judge≠critic mesh
   - "No more lost progress on crash" → preserve_on_fail worktrees + ledger replay
   - "No more 'where did this number come from?'" → INV-15 Z3-verified bounded-staleness
4. **Trust badges**: `[INV-15 ✓ Z3-verified]` `[SHA-256 ledger ✓ replay-verifiable]`
5. **6-principle manifesto** (link to PRINCIPLES.md)
6. **Capabilities grid** (8 primitives × HTTP endpoint each):
   - Decomposer · POST /api/decompose
   - Scheduler · POST /api/dispatch
   - Verification Mesh · GET /api/verify/:taskId
   - Ledger · GET /api/ledger/:runId
   - Consolidator · POST /api/consolidate
   - CLI Wrappers · `apohara orchestration send/check/...`
   - GitHub Bridge · webhook + poller
   - Tauri UI · localhost:7331
7. **5-stage lifecycle**: Specify → Decompose → Verify → Consolidate → Ship (with code snippet per stage)
8. **Use cases table** (3 concrete scenarios)
9. **Quick start** (Homebrew + curl|sh + source)
10. **Architecture diagram** (link to ARCHITECTURE.md)
11. **Footer nav**: Docs · Architecture · Roadmap · Paper (INV-15) · Discord · License · Changelog

### Task 11.7 — PRINCIPLES.md (6-principle manifesto)

```markdown
# What Drives Apohara

1. **Verifiability over vibes** — Every decision is replayable. Every claim has evidence. No "looks right to me."

2. **Locks over hopes** — Two agents can never overwrite each other's work. The coordinator's semantic conflict matrix is enforced, not aspired to.

3. **Audit over trust** — Cryptographic SHA-256 hash chain over every event. `apohara replay --verify` is the source of truth.

4. **Local-first over cloud** — Your subscriptions, your machine, your data. Optional GPU sidecar (ContextForge) only when you have the hardware.

5. **Wrappers over keys** — We wrap your existing Claude Code / Codex / OpenCode CLIs. Zero API keys. Your TOS, your rate limits.

6. **Formal over folklore** — The INV-15 JCR Safety Gate has a Z3 SMT formal proof. Critical invariants are PROVEN, not asserted.
```

### Task 11.8 — CHANGELOG.md v1.0.0 entry

Per spec §6 + Keep-A-Changelog format. Sections:
- **Added**: agent-hooks HTTP loopback, orchestration DB SQLite, BaseAgentProvider + ProtocolInterface refactor, 4 internal MCP servers, github-bridge poll mode, SPEC.md parser, two-tier transcript, runner execution policy presets, dual-path acceptance criteria, hallucination flag, strategy rotation anti-loop, …
- **Changed**: roster hardened to 3 CLI drivers (claude/codex/opencode); legacy 22 providers behind `APOHARA_LEGACY_PROVIDERS=1`
- **Deprecated**: webhook receive mode (use poll-only for v1.0; receive returns 501)
- **Removed**: nothing — legacy providers retained behind env flag
- **Fixed**: (whatever surfaces during Stages 1-10 implementation)
- **Security**: env sanitizer + PathSafety symlink-escape + bash compound splitter + per-worktree userData isolation

Link to `PRINCIPLES.md` + `docs/cloud-boundary.md`.

### Task 11.9 — ARCHITECTURE.md update

Reflect Stages 1-10 architecture: workspace layout (~30 crates + TS packages), three state machines (orchestration claim / run lifecycle / external tracker), agent-hooks loopback flow diagram, 4 internal MCP servers diagram, github-bridge poll flow, dispatch preamble pattern.

### Task 11.10 — Paper arXiv submission (manual — Pablo does it)

Per spec §8.5. Pablo's manual checklist:
1. Verify `apohara-context-forge/paper/inv15_paper.pdf` v3.0 in green CI.
2. Generate arXiv-friendly LaTeX (figures inline, bibliography style per arXiv).
3. Upload via arXiv web UI.
4. Once arXiv ID assigned: update `apohara-context-forge/paper/zenodo-v3-metadata.json` with `related_identifiers: [{ relation: "isVersionOf", identifier: "arxiv:XXXX.XXXXX", scheme: "arxiv" }]`.
5. Commit + push to `Apohara_Context_Forge` repo.
6. Update Apohara `CHANGELOG.md` v1.0.0 entry with arXiv ID hyperlink.

This task is the P-1 acceptance criterion. Apohara v1.0 is not considered "shipped" until arXiv ID is documented.

### Task 11.11 — Cloud boundary doc

`docs/cloud-boundary.md` per spec §11 / agentrail #16 inspiration:

```markdown
# Apohara — OSS vs Future Cloud Boundary

## OSS (always free, MIT)
- Orchestrator (local Tauri desktop)
- All 4 internal MCP servers
- All CLI wrapper providers
- Ledger + replay
- Verification mesh
- Worktree coordinator
- SPEC.md parser
- All Rust crates

## Future Cloud (hypothetical, undated)
- Hosted multi-machine daemon mode (Stage v1.1+, multica-inspired)
- Governed cross-attempt memory across teams
- Hosted GitHub App (operated product)
- Team audit log dashboards
- Enterprise SSO/RBAC/SCIM
- SLA + compliance

## Off-limits (NEVER moves to Cloud-only)
- Ledger SHA-256 chain — stays LOCAL-FIRST always
- CLI wrapper providers — stay LOCAL always (TOS requirement)
- Spec parser — stays LOCAL
- Replay verifier — stays LOCAL
```

### Task 11.12 — Stage 11 release checklist

```bash
# 1. Verify all 10 prior stages tagged
git tag | grep ^stage-

# 2. Run full setup verification
apohara verify-setup
apohara doctor --json | jq '.status == "ok"'

# 3. ContextForge regression
cd apohara-context-forge && PYTHONPATH=. pytest tests/ -q  # expect "310 passed"

# 4. Tag pre-release
git tag v1.0.0-rc.1
git push --tags  # triggers .github/workflows/desktop-release.yml

# 5. Beta test (1-2 weeks) on alpha channel

# 6. Promote to stable
apohara release promote v1.0.0
# This flips the same release prerelease=false, rebuilds RELEASE_NOTES.md

# 7. Publish Homebrew formula
# CI tagger updates packaging/homebrew/apohara.rb with real SHA256s and pushes to SuarezPM/homebrew-tap

# 8. Smoke test install paths
docker run --rm -i ubuntu:24.04 bash -c "curl -fsSL ... | sh && apohara --version"
docker run --rm -i fedora:41 bash -c "curl -fsSL ... | sh && apohara --version"
# macOS: brew install suarezpm/tap/apohara

# 9. Paper arXiv submission (manual)
# See Task 11.10 checklist

# 10. Tag stable
git tag v1.0.0
git push --tags

# 11. Announce
git commit --allow-empty -m "release: Apohara v1.0.0 shipped 🎉"
```

## Execution Handoff

**Plan complete and saved to `docs/superpowers/plans/2026-05-22-apohara-v1.md`.**

The plan covers 11 Stages, ~221 total tasks. Stages 1-3 are fully detailed with TDD steps. Stages 4-11 mix detailed leading tasks with compressed follow-up tasks for brevity (each compressed task has goal + files + acceptance criteria + 1-2 critical code snippets, which is enough for a competent engineer to expand inline using the prior tasks as template).

**Estimated implementation: 25-30 sprints solo-dev** (~6-8 months calendar with partial dedication).

**Two execution options:**

**1. Subagent-Driven (recommended)** — I dispatch a fresh subagent per task, review between tasks, fast iteration. Best for the detailed tasks (Stages 1-3 + heavy lifters in 4); the compressed tasks need the engineer to first expand them inline before dispatching.

**2. Inline Execution** — Execute tasks in this session using `superpowers:executing-plans`, batch execution with checkpoints for review. Best when you want to keep the context tight and review every few tasks.

**Which approach?** (Or do you want to take a break to read the plan first?)
